  2463. # [21:55] <@bz> Note that when working with JS you can have weird shit like this:
  2464. # [21:55] <@bz> var timer = createTimer();
  2465. # [21:55] * armenzg_brb is now known as armenzg
  2466. # [21:55] <@bz> timer.init(function() { /* do stuff */, 0, 0);
  2467. # [21:56] <@bz> And after that whether the timer fires depends on two things:
  2468. # [21:56] <@bz> (assuming the above is in a function, not at global scope)
  2469. # [21:56] <@bz> 1) GC timing
  2470. # [21:56] <@bz> 2) Exactly what "do stuff" does.
  2471. # [21:57] <espindola> ok, 1 I guessed from the restriction on having to keep the timer
  2472. # [21:57] <espindola> but 2?
  2473. # [21:57] <espindola> oh, if it causes a closure?

  2475. # [21:57] <espindola> that includes the timer ...
  2476. # [21:57] <@bz> Right

  2478. # [21:57] * jgriffin-afk is now known as jgriffin
